vxl-devel in Fedora 32

This page displays detailed information for a specific version of vxl-devel. You might want go back to the main page of vxl-devel.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2020-01-31 Fedora Release Engineering - 2.0.2-7 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_32_Mass_Rebuild
2019-09-15 Ankur Sinha - 2.0.2-6 - Fix failing build: update patch to fix minizip include
2019-07-27 Fedora Release Engineering - 2.0.2-5 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_31_Mass_Rebuild
2019-05-28 Ankur Sinha - 2.0.2-4 - Remove obsolete boxm library (was also causing arm build to fail) - Remove obsolete octree library
2019-05-28 Ankur Sinha - 2.0.2-3 - Fix 32 bit arch builds: https://github.com/vxl/vxl/issues/638 - Remove invalid comments - Do not make docs require the base package
2019-04-26 Ankur Sinha - 2.0.2-2 - Add complete file list - Remove no longer needed BR: klt - Remove more unneeded patches - Add patch to include FindRPLY.cmake - Use system shapelib and expat - More patches to complete build - Document failing tests, do not let them fail build
2019-04-19 Ankur Sinha - 2.0.2-2 - Enable OUL---why was it disabled? - Remove rply include patch: build seems to find it just fine. - Remove uneeded rply function call fix patch. - Remove Coin3D cmake config patch---included in cmake distribution now. - Remove SIMVoleon cmake patch---seems to find it just fine. - Correct CMake flags. - Enable BRL build - add Python BR - Add expatpp bits manually - File upstream issue and use bundled openjpeg2: https://github.com/vxl/vxl/issues/627 - Remove unneeded xerces BR, and corresponding patch.
2019-04-18 Ankur Sinha - 2.0.2-1 - Update to latest upstream release - Temporarily use bundled dcmtk (https://github.com/vxl/vxl/issues/550) - Use new github upstream - Remove uneeded patches - Explicitly list all shared objects
2019-03-09 Antonio Trande - 1.17.0-31 - Rebuild for dcmtk-3.6.4
2019-02-17 Ankur Sinha - 1.17.0-30 - Use autosetup macro - Remove whitespaces, use space instead of tabs for cleanliness
